like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . tell your doctor immediately if you experience : - weakness , feel light - headed or dizzy or have difficulty breathing , as these may be signs of a serious allergic reaction . - if you develop a combination of any of the following symptoms : - weakness or light - headedness , dizzy or difficulty breathing , as these may be signs of a serious allergic reaction . - if you develop a combination of any of the following symptoms : - weakness or light - headedness , stop taking this medicine and contact your doctor straight away . - severe allergic reactions ( e . g . stevens - johnson syndrome , toxic epidermal necrolysis , erythema multiforme , drug reaction with eosinophilia and systemic symptoms [ dress ]), see section 2 . tell your doctor immediately if you develop a combination of any of the following symptoms : - swelling of the face , lips , mouth , tongue and / or throat and difficulty breathing . contact your doctor immediately if you notice any of the following signs of diabetic ketoacidosis ( see also section " warnings and precautions "). - swelling in the mouth , mouth , tongue or throat , which may cause difficulty in swallowing or swallowing , stop taking this medicine and talk to your doctor as soon as possible . - if you notice any of the above or combination of the following side effects : severe and persistent pain in the abdomen ( stomach area ) which might reach through to your ankles , as these may indicate problems with your ovaries ( peripheral neuropathy ). - severe allergic reactions ( eosinophilia , anaphylactic reaction , eosinophilia and systemic symptoms [ dress ]), see section 2 . tell your doctor immediately if you experience any of the following symptoms : - swelling of the face , lips , mouth , tongue and / or throat that may cause difficulty in swallowing or breathing , as this could be a sign of a serious allergic reaction . - if you develop a combination of any of these symptoms , contact your doctor as soon as possible . - if you have a combination of any of the following symptoms : - weakness or weakness , especially if you feel light - headed or dizzy or have difficulty breathing , as these may be signs of a serious allergic reaction ( e . g . stevens - johnson syndrome , toxic epidermal necrolysis , erythema multiforme , drug reaction with eosinophilia and systemic symptoms [ dress ]), see section 2 . tell your doctor immediately if you experience any of the following signs of diabetic ketoacidosis ( see also section " warnings and precautions ): - swelling in the mouth , throat , nose , genitals and eyes and can be preceded by a_high_temperature . - severe allergic reactions ( eosinophilia and systemic symptoms [ dress ]), see section 2 . - flu - like symptoms , which can appear as reddish target - like macules or circular patches often with central blisters on the trunk , skin peeling , ulcers of mouth , throat , nose , genitals and eyes and can be preceded by eosinophilia and flu - like symptoms . stop using levetiracetam_actavis if you develop these symptoms and contact your doctor or seek medical attention immediately . see also section 2 . - if you notice any of these symptoms , contact your doctor as soon as possible . reporting of side effects if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in levetiracetam_actavis appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
